30  import java.nio.charset.Charset;
31  import java.nio.charset.CharsetDecoder;
32  import java.nio.charset.CharsetEncoder;
33  import java.nio.charset.CharacterCodingException;
34  import sun.nio.cs.HistoricallyNamedCharset;
35  import sun.nio.cs.ext.*;
36  
37  
38  public class IBM942_OLD extends Charset implements HistoricallyNamedCharset
39  {
40  
41      public IBM942_OLD() {
42          super("x-IBM942-Old", null);
43      }
44  
45      public String historicalName() {
46          return "Cp942";
47      }
48  
49      public boolean contains(Charset cs) {
50          return (cs instanceof IBM942);
51      }
52  
53      public CharsetDecoder newDecoder() {
54          return new Decoder(this);
55      }
56  
57      public CharsetEncoder newEncoder() {
58          return new Encoder(this);
59      }
60  
61  
62      public short[] getDecoderIndex1() {
63          return Decoder.index1;
64  
65      }
66      public String getDecoderIndex2() {
67          return Decoder.index2;
68  
69      }
70      public short[] getEncoderIndex1() {
71          return Encoder.index1;
72  
73      }
74      public String getEncoderIndex2() {
75          return Encoder.index2;
76  
77      }
78      public String getEncoderIndex2a() {
79          return Encoder.index2a;
80  
81      }
82  
83      protected static class Decoder extends DBCS_IBM_ASCII_Decoder {
84  
85          private void initLookupTables() {
86              super.mask1 = 0xFFC0;
87              super.mask2 = 0x003F;
88              super.shift = 6;
89              super.leadByte = this.leadByte;
90              super.index1 = this.index1;
91              super.index2 = this.index2;
92          }
93  
94          public Decoder(Charset cs) {
95                  super(cs);
96                  super.singleByteToChar = this.singleByteToChar;
97                  initLookupTables();
98          }
99  
100         protected Decoder(Charset cs, String singleByteToChar) {
101                 super(cs);
102                 super.singleByteToChar = singleByteToChar;
103                 initLookupTables();
104         }
